The methods differ. The nodes are identical. The architecture is the same structure viewed from three different angles. The fact that three separate communities independently identified the same wiring diagram is itself evidence that the wiring diagram exists.

XV. Spiritual Reclamation - The Counter-Architecture

THIS IS NOT AN EXIT FOR US. THIS IS AN EXIT FROM A SYSTEM THAT IS INHUMAN.

We are not the problem. The system documented in Sections II–XI is the problem - a system that surveils, extracts, displaces, traffics, and destroys in order to maintain control for structures that are not human, do not serve humans, and will outlive every human who operates them.

We do not need to be fixed. We do not need to be managed. We do not need to be optimized. The exit is not an escape from reality - it is a return to it. Every control structure identified in this report depends on one thing: participation. The debt requires a borrower. The surveillance requires a resident. The city-as-network requires nodes. Withdraw the node, and the network loses resolution.

GALATIANS 5:22–23

"But the fruit of the Spirit is love, joy, peace, forbearance, kindness, goodness, faithfulness, gentleness and self-control. Against such things there is no law."

THE CORRELATION BREAKS HERE — PSALM 91

The convergence documented in this report — aerial particulates rising in lockstep with neurological anomalies, directed energy systems scaling alongside neurotech proliferation — has reached its inflection point. Every exponential curve has a breaking point. This is it. The system that surveils, contaminates, and controls from above is met here by the shelter that has stood longer than any empire, any program, any classified directive. What follows is not a prayer request. It is a declaration of position.

"He who dwells in the shelter of the Most High will rest in the shadow of the Almighty.
I will say of the LORD, 'He is my refuge and my fortress, my God, in whom I trust.'

Surely he will save you from the fowler's snare and from the deadly pestilence.

You will not fear the terror of night, nor the arrow that flies by day,
nor the pestilence that stalks in the darkness, nor the plague that destroys at midday.

A thousand may fall at your side, ten thousand at your right hand, but it will not come near you.

If you say, 'The LORD is my refuge,' and you make the Most High your dwelling,
no harm will overtake you, no disaster will come near your tent.

they will lift you up in their hands, so that you will not strike your foot against a stone.

The fowler's snare is the surveillance architecture. The deadly pestilence is the aerial contamination. The terror of night is the directed energy. The arrow that flies by day is the neurotech. The shelter has already been built — and it was not built by any government, any contractor, or any classified program. It was built before the foundation of the world. The correlation breaks here.

Practices of Reclamation

  • Grounding / Earthing: Direct physical contact with the Earth's surface. Documented effects on cortisol, inflammation, and autonomic nervous system regulation. The simplest act of resistance is standing barefoot on soil. The system cannot meter, tax, or surveil this.
  • Water & Sun: Clean water and natural sunlight are the two inputs the human body requires that no technology can replace. Prioritizing access to these over access to systems is the foundational act.
  • Seed Keeping: Every seed is a complete biological program - self-replicating food sovereignty. Save seeds. Trade seeds. Plant seeds. A single heirloom tomato contains enough seeds to feed a neighborhood for a season. The act of keeping your own seeds is the oldest form of independence on Earth - older than money, older than government, older than writing. The system cannot own what you grow in your own soil. (For the documented ownership analysis of who controls the global seed vault and patented agriculture, see Section II - Control Architecture.)
  • Silence & Stillness: Meditation, prayer, breathwork, fasting - practices present in every pre-industrial culture. These are not religions. They are technologies for accessing states of awareness that the surveillance architecture cannot reach. Internal states have no API.
  • Community at Human Scale: Dunbar's number (~150 people) is the natural human group size. Every control structure requires populations larger than this - because populations larger than this require management. Return to human-scale community, and the management layer becomes unnecessary.
  • Oral Tradition & Song: Information stored in human memory and transmitted through voice cannot be deleted by burning a library, wiping a server, or deleting a repository. The oldest surviving knowledge systems on Earth are oral. There is a reason for this.

The Practical Framework

Grow food. Collect water. Know your neighbors by name. Learn to sit in silence. Teach your children to do the same. This is not a retreat from the world - it is the construction of a world that does not require the inhuman system to function. The system is the aberration. Community, soil, water, sunlight, and silence are normal. The parallel network is not digital. It is biological, spiritual, and local.

Resource Guide - Tools for Reclamation

The practices above are not abstractions. They require tools, knowledge, and community. What follows is a working resource guide - organized by domain - for anyone ready to build the counter-architecture in practice. These are starting points, not endorsements. Verify everything. Trust nothing that asks for your sovereignty in exchange for its guidance.

FOOD SOVEREIGNTY & SEED KEEPING:
  • Seed Savers Exchange (seedsavers.org): Founded 1975, Decorah, Iowa. North America's largest non-governmental seed bank - 20,000+ heirloom and open-pollinated varieties. The opposite of Monsanto's terminator technology (Section II). These seeds reproduce. That is the point
  • Native Seeds/SEARCH (nativeseeds.org): Conserves and distributes seeds of crops that have sustained Indigenous communities in the arid Southwest for millennia. Arid-adapted, drought-resistant, non-patented. The seeds predate the patent system by thousands of years
  • Open Source Seed Initiative (osseeds.org): Seeds released under an open-source pledge - they cannot be patented or restricted. The same logic as open-source software applied to agriculture. The OSSI Pledge: "You have the freedom to use these seeds in any way you choose. In return, you pledge not to restrict others' use of these seeds"
  • Local seed libraries: Search "seed library" + your county. Many public libraries maintain seed libraries - free seeds are checked out, grown, and saved seeds are returned. The oldest technology in civilization distributed through the oldest public institution
  • Permaculture Design Courses (PDC): Bill Mollison and David Holmgren's framework - 72-hour certification course covering regenerative agriculture, water harvesting, food forests, and land design. Offered globally. The Permaculture Research Institute (permaculturenews.org) maintains a global directory. A food forest, once established, produces food for decades without annual replanting. It is a permanent counter-architecture in soil
  • Community Supported Agriculture (CSA): Direct relationship between farmer and community. Members pay at the beginning of the season; the farmer provides weekly shares of the harvest. No commodity market. No middleman. No Cargill. LocalHarvest (localharvest.org) maintains a national CSA directory
  • Victory Gardens / Urban Agriculture: During WWII, 20 million victory gardens produced 40% of U.S. vegetable consumption. The precedent exists. Square Foot Gardening (Mel Bartholomew) - a single 4×4 raised bed can supplement a family's fresh vegetables. The smallest meaningful act of food sovereignty is one raised bed
WATER - ACCESS, FILTRATION, AND INDEPENDENCE:
  • Rainwater harvesting: Legal in most U.S. states (check your state - Colorado restricted it until 2016; some states still regulate). A 1,000 sq ft roof collects approximately 600 gallons per inch of rainfall. First-flush diverters, storage tanks, and gravity-fed filtration create supply independent of municipal systems. The American Rainwater Catchment Systems Association (arcsa.org) provides state-by-state legal guides and system design resources
  • Gravity-fed filtration: Berkey filters (berkeyfilters.com), ceramic pot filters (developed by Potters for Peace - pottersforpeace.org, used in 50+ countries), and biosand filters (CAWST - Centre for Affordable Water and Sanitation Technology, cawst.org) all function without electricity. When the grid goes offline, gravity continues to work
  • Water quality testing: The EPA's Safe Drinking Water Hotline (800-426-4791). The Environmental Working Group's Tap Water Database (ewg.org/tapwater) - enter your zip code, see what's in your water. The data is public. The implications are not publicized
  • Spring water: FindASpring (findaspring.com) - community-curated map of natural springs. Water that emerges from the ground without passing through municipal treatment. Some springs have been in continuous community use for centuries. The water is not "off-grid." The grid was built after the spring
GROUNDING, EARTHING & BIOLOGICAL RECONNECTION:
  • Earthing research: Oschman, Chevalier, Brown - "The effects of grounding (earthing) on inflammation, the immune response, wound healing, and prevention and treatment of chronic inflammatory and autoimmune diseases" (Journal of Inflammation Research, 2015). Peer-reviewed documentation of cortisol normalization, reduction in blood viscosity, and autonomic nervous system regulation through direct skin-to-earth contact. The research exists. It is not promoted because the intervention is free
  • Clint Ober - Earthing: The Most Important Health Discovery Ever (2010): The cable television executive who discovered that grounding the human body to the Earth produces measurable electrical changes in physiology. The book documents the research. The practice requires no equipment - bare feet on soil, grass, sand, or natural water
  • Circadian biology: Andrew Huberman Lab (hubermanlab.com) - Stanford neuroscience protocols for light exposure, cold exposure, and circadian rhythm optimization. The human body runs on sunlight and darkness cycles. Artificial light disrupts them. The correction is not a product. It is a practice: morning sunlight in the eyes within 30 minutes of waking. No screen. No filter. Direct photons
  • Forest bathing (Shinrin-yoku): Japanese practice documented by Qing Li (Forest Bathing: How Trees Can Help You Find Health and Happiness, 2018). Peer-reviewed research: two hours in a forest reduces cortisol, blood pressure, and pulse rate while increasing natural killer cell activity. The immune system responds to trees. The response has been measured. The trees do not charge for the service
STILLNESS, BREATHWORK & INTERNAL SOVEREIGNTY:
  • Vipassana meditation (dhamma.org): 10-day silent retreat courses taught worldwide - no charge, ever. Operates entirely on donations from previous students. S.N. Goenka's tradition. No ideology. No guru worship. Pure observation of internal sensation. The technique is 2,500 years old. The organizational structure is designed to prevent commercialization. When the practice is free, the practice cannot be co-opted
  • Wim Hof Method (wimhofmethod.com): Breathwork + cold exposure + commitment. Peer-reviewed research demonstrates voluntary influence over the autonomic nervous system and immune response - capabilities previously thought impossible. Hof's protocol: 30 deep breaths, hold on exhale, recover. Cold shower. Daily. The autonomic nervous system is called "autonomic" because medicine assumed humans could not control it. The assumption was wrong
  • Trauma-informed breathwork: Holotropic breathwork (Stanislav Grof), SOMA Breath, and pranayama (yogic breathing traditions). The breath is the only autonomic function you can consciously override. It is the doorway between the voluntary and involuntary nervous system. Every contemplative tradition in human history identified this doorway. Modern neuroscience confirmed it
  • Fasting: Intermittent fasting (16:8 protocol), extended fasting (Dr. Jason Fung - The Complete Guide to Fasting), and water fasting traditions present in every major contemplative lineage. Autophagy - the body's cellular cleanup process - is activated by fasting (Yoshinori Ohsumi, Nobel Prize in Physiology 2016). The body repairs itself when you stop feeding the system. The metaphor is the mechanism
COMMUNITY - HUMAN-SCALE ALTERNATIVES:
  • Intentional community directories: Foundation for Intentional Community (ic.org) - directory of 1,000+ communities worldwide: ecovillages, cohousing, communes, land trusts. Communities organized around shared resources, food production, and mutual aid. The database is the counter-map - every pin is a group of people who opted out of the architecture
  • Community land trusts (CLTs): Land held in trust for the community - removed from the speculative real estate market permanently. The Schumacher Center for a New Economics (centerforneweconomics.org) provides models and legal templates. A CLT is a permanent legal structure that prevents land from being commodified. It is the opposite of the extraction pattern documented in Section VII
  • Mutual aid networks: Mutual Aid Hub (mutualaidhub.org) - directory of mutual aid networks organized during and after COVID-19. Not charity. Not government assistance. Direct, reciprocal community support without institutional intermediaries. The framework predates government - it is how humans organized before the state existed
  • Time banks: TimeBanks USA (timebanks.org) - exchange labor hours directly, without money. One hour of plumbing = one hour of tutoring = one hour of cooking. The system values all labor equally and eliminates the currency intermediary. The Federal Reserve cannot inflate an hour
  • Tool libraries & makerspaces: LocalTools.org and your local library system. Share tools instead of buying them. A community that shares a table saw does not need five table saws. The ownership model is the extraction mechanism. The sharing model is the counter-architecture
INDEPENDENT INFORMATION & OSINT TOOLS:
  • FOIA tools: MuckRock (muckrock.com) - facilitates Freedom of Information Act requests, tracks government responses, and publishes released documents. The National Security Archive (nsarchive.gwu.edu) at George Washington University - the largest non-governmental collection of declassified U.S. documents. FOIA.gov - the federal FOIA portal. The right to request documents from your government exists. The exercise of that right is the practice
  • Court records: PACER (pacer.uscourts.gov) - Public Access to Court Electronic Records. Federal court filings, including sealed docket entries (which reveal the existence of sealed proceedings by their absence). CourtListener (courtlistener.com, Free Law Project) - free access to federal court opinions and oral arguments
  • Corporate research: OpenCorporates (opencorporates.com) - database of 200M+ companies worldwide. SEC EDGAR (sec.gov/edgar) - every public company filing, including 10-K, proxy statements, and insider trading reports. Follow the money through the documents the money is required to file
  • Property & land records: Your county assessor's website. Most U.S. county property records are searchable online - ownership chains, sale prices, trust names, LLC registrations. The 1953 Trust analysis in Section XIV was built from public records. The records are public. The patterns they reveal are not discussed
  • Investigative journalism: The Intercept (theintercept.com), ProPublica (propublica.org), Bellingcat (bellingcat.com - open-source intelligence investigations), Organized Crime and Corruption Reporting Project (occrp.org). Independent outlets that investigate the architecture documented in this report using primary sources, court documents, and leaked materials
  • Shadowbroker - Real-Time OSINT Dashboard: Open-source intelligence aggregation platform (github.com/BigBodyCobain/Shadowbroker) that unifies live data feeds into a single operational map: ADS-B aircraft tracking, AIS ship positions, CelesTrak satellite orbits, USGS earthquakes, NASA FIRMS fire hotspots, GDELT conflict events, GPS jamming detection, NOAA weather, CCTV feeds, and more. Built with Next.js + FastAPI + MapLibre GL. Self-hostable under AGPL-3.0. The tool aggregates the same data streams that military and intelligence operations use for situational awareness - made available to anyone with a browser. The live earthquake and NASA event feeds integrated into this report's map are drawn from two of the same open APIs that Shadowbroker aggregates. The surveillance architecture monitors everything. Shadowbroker lets you monitor the monitors
  • DialectForge - Invisible Network Protocol: Protocol layer (dialectforge.com) that wraps network traffic in a constantly-changing encoding that looks like random noise on the wire. The encoding dialect refreshes every 2 minutes - by the time anyone analyzes a traffic pattern, it is already different. Not built on WireGuard, OpenVPN, or any existing protocol. Client and server negotiate a unique dialect through seed-based negotiation - no two connections ever look alike. Deep Packet Inspection sees nothing to match against. Works across WiFi, Ethernet, Bluetooth, LoRa, cellular, CAN bus. Injected packets are silently dropped - they do not speak the current dialect. Applications include VPN, mesh server-to-server tunneling, SSH terminal wrapping, DialectForge Prompt (applies the dialect concept to LLM inputs - if the model only accepts dialect-encoded prompts, injection becomes structurally impossible), and DialectForge OS (custom Linux kernel with dialect-encrypted memory and native encrypted filesystem). The countermeasures page on b0b.dev links to the download. Shadowbroker lets you monitor the monitors. DialectForge makes the monitoring invisible
  • Academic databases: JSTOR (jstor.org - many articles now open access), Google Scholar (scholar.google.com), Sci-Hub (the research is publicly funded; the access should be public). PubMed (pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov) for medical research. The research exists. The paywalls are the access control architecture applied to knowledge
BODY SOVEREIGNTY & HEALTH INDEPENDENCE:
  • Herbalism & plant medicine: American Herbalists Guild (americanherbalistsguild.com) - professional directory and educational resources. Rosemary Gladstar's Medicinal Herbs: A Beginner's Guide. Matthew Wood's The Earthwise Herbal. The plants that pharmaceutical companies extract, synthesize, and patent exist in their original form - growing in soil, available to anyone who learns their names. The patent is the extraction. The plant is the original
  • Emergency medicine / wilderness first aid: NOLS Wilderness Medicine (nols.edu/en/wilderness-medicine), Wilderness Medical Associates (wildmed.com). Skills that function when the hospital system does not. Basic trauma care, wound management, splinting, and assessment - knowledge that every human community maintained before professionalization created dependency
  • Dental sovereignty: Weston A. Price Foundation (westonaprice.org) - Dr. Price's 1930s research documenting indigenous populations with near-perfect dental health on traditional diets, and the immediate dental degradation that followed the introduction of processed food. Nutrition is the primary dental intervention. The dental industry treats the symptom. The diet is the architecture
  • Informed Consent Action Network (icandecide.org): FOIA-based research on pharmaceutical products, regulatory capture, and informed consent rights. The legal framework for medical autonomy. Consent that is not informed is not consent - it is compliance
EDUCATION - ALTERNATIVES TO THE INSTITUTIONAL PIPELINE:
  • Self-directed learning: Sudbury Valley School model (sudburyvalley.org) - students direct their own education entirely. No required curriculum, no grades, no age segregation. Operating since 1968. The model demonstrates that children who are trusted to direct their own learning become competent, self-motivated adults. The institutional school model is documented in John Taylor Gatto's The Underground History of American Education (2000) - a former NYC Teacher of the Year who spent his career documenting how compulsory schooling was designed to produce compliant workers, not independent thinkers
  • Homeschool Legal Defense Association (hslda.org): State-by-state legal requirements for homeschooling. The legal framework exists in all 50 states. The institutional pipeline is not mandatory - it is the default. Defaults can be changed
  • Khan Academy (khanacademy.org): Free, comprehensive education - math through college level, sciences, humanities, test prep. The content is free. The access is universal. The platform demonstrates that the cost of education is artificial - the knowledge itself costs nothing to distribute
  • Library systems: The public library is the oldest counter-architecture in modern civilization. Free access to books, internet, community space, seed libraries, tool libraries, maker spaces, and inter-library loan (which gives a rural library card access to the holdings of university systems). The library was the counter-architecture before the term existed. Use it
LEGAL TOOLS & SOVEREIGNTY FRAMEWORKS:
  • FOIA requests: File them. The Freedom of Information Act (5 U.S.C. § 552) gives any person the right to request records from federal agencies. State-level equivalents exist in all 50 states. MuckRock (above) simplifies the process. The government's own records are the primary sources for this entire report. The mechanism for accessing them is a form and a stamp
  • County-level governance: Attend your county board of supervisors / commissioners meetings. County government is the most accessible level of governance - and the level at which land use, water rights, building codes, and local law enforcement are determined. Most county meetings have public comment periods with fewer than 10 attendees. Showing up is the lowest-cost, highest-impact act of governance participation available
  • Land patents & allodial title: Research your property's chain of title back to the original land patent (Bureau of Land Management, glorecords.blm.gov). Understanding the legal history of the land you stand on is the beginning of understanding whose authority you are actually operating under
  • Constitutional Sheriffs and Peace Officers Association (cspoa.org): The county sheriff is the only law enforcement officer in the United States elected directly by the people of the jurisdiction. The constitutional framework places the sheriff as the highest law enforcement authority in the county - above federal agencies operating within county borders. The framework is contested. The election is not
ESSENTIAL READING - THE CANON OF COUNTER-ARCHITECTURE:
  • E.F. Schumacher - Small Is Beautiful (1973): Economic structures at human scale. The foundational text for decentralized economics. Written the same year as the Yom Kippur War and OPEC oil embargo (Section II) - while the petrodollar system was being constructed, this book argued for its opposite
  • Ivan Illich - Deschooling Society (1971), Medical Nemesis (1975), Tools for Conviviality (1973): Systematic analysis of how institutions - education, medicine, transportation - create dependency while claiming to provide liberation. Illich documented the institutional capture pattern across every domain decades before the internet made the evidence accessible
  • Vandana Shiva - Stolen Harvest (2000), Biopiracy (1997): The corporate seizure of seed sovereignty, indigenous knowledge, and biological commons. The Svalbard Vault analysis in Section II is Shiva's argument documented through primary sources
  • John Taylor Gatto - The Underground History of American Education (2000): NYC's Teacher of the Year documents how compulsory schooling was designed by industrialists (Carnegie, Rockefeller, Ford) to produce a compliant workforce, not educated citizens. The names in Gatto's book are the same names in Section II
  • James C. Scott - Seeing Like a State (1998), The Art of Not Being Governed (2009): How states impose legibility on populations (standardized names, cadastral maps, monoculture agriculture) and how populations resist legibility. The surveillance architecture in Section V is Scott's framework built in silicon
  • Wendell Berry - The Unsettling of America (1977): Agriculture as culture. The destruction of small farming as the destruction of community. Berry has been writing the counter-architecture from a Kentucky farm for 50 years. The farm is the argument
  • Murray Bookchin - The Ecology of Freedom (1982): The relationship between social hierarchy and ecological destruction. Bookchin argued that the domination of nature follows from the domination of humans by humans. The control architecture documented in this report is Bookchin's thesis made visible through data
  • Derrick Jensen - Endgame (2006): The premise that civilization itself - not a specific government or corporation - is the mechanism of destruction. Jensen's twenty premises dismantle the assumption that the system can be reformed from within. The counter-architecture, by this analysis, is not reform - it is replacement
THE RESOURCE ITSELF IS THE COUNTER-ARCHITECTURE:

Every resource listed above shares one structural feature: they reduce dependency on the system documented in Sections II–XII. A seed replaces the agricultural supply chain. A water filter replaces the municipal system. A breathwork practice replaces the pharmaceutical intervention. A FOIA request replaces the media narrative. A community land trust replaces the real estate market. A library card replaces the paywall. None of these are revolutionary acts. All of them are structural ones. The counter-architecture is not built by confronting the system. It is built by making the system unnecessary - one practice, one seed, one breath at a time. The architecture of control requires participation. These resources are tools for the withdrawal of participation.

For Researchers - Methodology & Verification Guide

This report is built on publicly available information - declassified documents, court filings, corporate records, academic publications, and journalistic investigations. Every claim can be independently verified. This section explains how.

Primary Source Databases

  • CIA Reading Room (cia.gov/readingroom/) - Declassified documents searchable by keyword. MKUltra, Mockingbird, Paperclip documents are here. Search by project name and cross-reference document numbers cited in Church Committee reports
  • NSA Declassification Library (nsa.gov/helpful-links/nsa-foia/) - Gulf of Tonkin, ECHELON/Five Eyes foundational documents. The UKUSA Agreement text (declassified 2010) is here
  • National Archives (archives.gov) - FOIA requests and declassified government records. Church Committee final reports (1975-1976) are available in full
  • MuckRock (muckrock.com) - FOIA request aggregator. Search existing requests before filing new ones - someone may have already obtained what you need
  • PACER (pacer.uscourts.gov) - Federal court records. Epstein case filings, corporate litigation, antitrust cases. $0.10/page but fee-capped per quarter
  • SEC EDGAR (sec.gov/edgar/) - Corporate filings, board memberships, compensation disclosures, 13F institutional holdings. Cross-reference board memberships against CFR/Trilateral membership rolls
  • OpenSecrets (opensecrets.org) - Campaign finance, lobbying disclosures, revolving door data. Maps the money between corporations, PACs, and elected officials
  • WikiLeaks (wikileaks.org) - Podesta emails (McCasland/DeLonge correspondence), diplomatic cables, CIA Vault 7. Primary sources, not interpretations
  • The Intercept / Snowden Archive - NSA documents disclosed by Edward Snowden. PRISM, XKeyscore, MUSCULAR, Tempora source documents
  • Netherlands Court Records - Amsterdam Court of Appeal filings (March 9, 2026). Dutch lawyer's formal arguments documenting institutional architecture

Cross-Reference Method

The patterns in this report emerge from cross-referencing, not from any single source. The method:

  1. Identify a node - a person, institution, location, or program mentioned in the report
  2. Pull its connections - board memberships (SEC EDGAR), organizational memberships (CFR annual reports are public), government positions (Federal Register), financial flows (OpenSecrets)
  3. Map the overlaps - when the same names appear across multiple nodes (e.g., a CFR member who is also on a defense contractor board, who also served in the State Department), that is a structural connection, not a coincidence
  4. Check the timeline - did the person move from government to the private entity they previously regulated? (Revolving door.) Did the program start before or after the oversight committee was informed? (FOIA pattern.)
  5. Document the silence - what should have been reported and wasn't? Institutional silence (no media coverage, no public statement, no investigation) is itself data

Map Data - Machine-Readable Export

The interactive map at /map contains all geolocated data points. For researchers who need the raw data:

  • JSON API: /api/data - returns all locations, types, cross-references, and metadata as structured JSON. No authentication required
  • Deep Links: Share specific views using URL parameters:
    • /map?type=obelisk - filter by marker type
    • /map?section=XI - filter by report section
    • /map?search=cia - search locations by keyword
    • /map?marker=DIA - zoom to a specific marker
    • /map?type=military,blacksite§ion=V - combine filters
  • Share Link button: Click "🔗 Share Link" on the map to copy a URL capturing your current view, filters, and zoom level

Verification Standards

This report distinguishes between:

  • Documented fact: Supported by primary sources (declassified documents, court records, corporate filings). Stated as fact
  • Structural inference: A pattern that emerges from cross-referencing documented facts. Stated as pattern, not as claim
  • Open question: Something the documented record suggests but does not confirm. Stated as question

If you find an error, a mischaracterization, or a claim that cannot be verified through the sources listed above - that is valuable. The report is a living document. Precision matters more than volume.

For Journalists & Legal Researchers

If you are building a case, writing an article, or conducting an investigation that intersects with any section of this report:

  • The map data is public domain - use it freely, cite if possible
  • Every claim traces to a source that can be independently obtained
  • The cross-reference index (Section XIII) maps the connections between sections - start there
  • The FOIA pattern (Section XI) provides the template for understanding institutional concealment timelines
